# Excalidraw Data

## Text Elements
since the first derivative is the gradient of the function, the points where the function is
flat have gradient 0 and therefore the first derivative is 0 ^iHItaiMQ

the number by which every element in a geometric sequence is multiplied ^CCyM1Ndt

sum of the terms of a sequence ^fPgecY0F
